In[222]:= e1[t_]:=-D[H[t],t]/H[t]^2
D[e1[t],t]/(H[t]e1[t])//FullSimplify
Out[223]= (-2 (H^′)[t]^2+H[t] (H^′′)[t])/(H[t]^2 (H^′)[t])
